				<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading pagetitle page-header">
					Prelude and Fugue in B-flat minor, BWV 867 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)				</h1>	

				<div class="body"><div lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr"><div class="wp_header">
<table>
<table>

<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composition Year
</th>
<td>1722 in <i><a href="/wiki/Das_wohltemperierte_Klavier_I,_BWV_846-869_(Bach,_Johann_Sebastian)" title="Das wohltemperierte Klavier I, BWV 846-869 (Bach, Johann Sebastian)">Das wohltemperierte Klavier I, BWV 846-869</a></i> (No.22)
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Genre Categories<span class="addpagetag mh555"></span>
</th>
<td><span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Preludes&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Preludes</a></span>; <span class="plainlinks"><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://imslp.org/index.php?title=Category:Fugues&amp;transclude=Template:Catintro">Fugues</a></span>;
